<script type="text/javascript">

// =============================================================================
// Function Class: Show/Hide product promotions & special offers link
// =============================================================================

function showElement(id) {
  var elm = document.getElementById(id);
  if (elm) {
    elm.style.visibility = 'visible';
    if (elm.getAttribute('name') == 'heroQuickPromoDiv') {
      elm.style.display = 'block';
    }
  }
}
function hideElement(id) {
  var elm = document.getElementById(id);
  if (elm) {
    elm.style.visibility = 'hidden';
    if (elm.getAttribute('name') == 'heroQuickPromoDiv') {
      elm.style.display = 'none';
    }
  }
}
function showHideElement(h_id, div_id) {
  var hiddenTag = document.getElementById(h_id);
  if (hiddenTag) {
    showElement(div_id);
  } else {
    hideElement(div_id);
  }
}

        if(b.e){amznJQ.completedStage(b.e);};

    }
}

  var old_error_handler = _onerror;

            ]
          }
  };

    function findMatch(f){
	for(var attribution in attributionMap){
	    var i=0;
	    var attributionValue = attributionMap[attribution];
	    var files = attributionValue['files'];
	    while(files[i]){
		if(f.match(files[i])){
	            var exception={};
		    exception.attribution = attribution;
		    if(attributionValue.hasOwnProperty("logLevel")){
			exception.logLevel = attributionValue['logLevel'];	
		    }
		return exception;
           	}
		i++;
	    }
        }
	return null;
    }


    function dpOnErrorOverride(message, file, line, col, error){
     var matchingErrorFound = false;
     if(typeof file == "string"){
        try{
	    var jsException = findMatch(file);
	    if(jsException && typeof jsException === "object"){
                jsException.m =  message;
                jsException.f = file;
                jsException.l = line;
                jsException.c =  "" + (col || "");
                jsException.err =  error;
                jsException.fromOnError = 1;
                jsException.args = arguments;
                if(window.ueLogError){
               	    window.ueLogError(jsException);
		    matchingErrorFound = true;
		    if(ue && ue.count){
		        ue.count("dpJavascriptAffectedErrors", (ue.count("dpJavascriptAffectedErrors") || 0) + 1);
		        ue.count("dpJSError" + jsException.attribution, (ue.count("dpJSError" + jsException.attribution) || 0) + 1);
		    }
	        }
            }
	}catch(exception){
	    if(window.ueLogError){
	        window.ueLogError(exception,{message: "dpOnErrorOverride: error occurred - ", logLevel:"FATAL"});
	    }
	}
    }
	if(!matchingErrorFound){ 
          old_error_handler.apply(this, arguments);
	}
        return false;
    }

      dpOnErrorOverride.skipTrace = 1;
      window.onerror = dpOnErrorOverride;
    })(window.onerror);

      dialogPINPC.PINRequested = (dialogPINPC.PINRequested)? false : true;

P.when('A').execute(function(A){
    var $ = A.$;

    var sendAnalytics = function(reftag) {
      if (reftag!=null) {
        $.ajax({
          url: "/gp/video/usdvm/ajax/analytics.html/ref="+reftag,
          data: {},
          dataType: "json",
          timeout: 10000
        });
      }
    };

    window.sendAnalytics = sendAnalytics;
});








var bindAvodAjaxTooltip = function(args) {
    if(typeof amznJQ !== 'undefined') {
        amznJQ.available('popover', function() {
            
            var playerWasVisible = false,
                escapedContent = args.text ? jQuery('<div/>').html(args.text).text() : '';

            jQuery(args.selector).amazonPopoverTrigger({
                showOnHover: false,
                destination: args.url,
                literalContent: escapedContent,
                showCloseButton: false,
                width: 400,
                ajaxErrorContent: '<p>We encountered a problem. Please try again.</p>',
                onShow: function() {
                    // hide player if present
                    amznJQ.onReady("webGlobalVideoPlayer.MainPlayerInitialized", function() {
                        amznJQ.onReady("dvwPlayerContainer", function() {
                            var mainPlayer = amzn.webGlobalVideoPlayer.getMainPlayer();
                            if (mainPlayer.isVisible()) {
                                playerWasVisible = true;
                                mainPlayer.close();
                            }
                        });
                    });
                },
                onHide: function() {
                    // show player and restart playback if needed
                    amznJQ.onReady("webGlobalVideoPlayer.MainPlayerInitialized", function() {
                        amznJQ.onReady("dvwPlayerContainer", function() {
                            var mainPlayer = amzn.webGlobalVideoPlayer.getMainPlayer();
                            if (playerWasVisible) {
                                mainPlayer.play();
                            }
                        });
                    });
                },
                closeEventInclude: "MOUSE_LEAVE"
            });
        });
    }
}

    var playerWasVisible = false,

var hideFlash = function() {
    jQuery("div#streamBoxTable div#streaming_container").css("background-color", "black")
        .find("#streaming").css("visibility", "hidden");
}
var showFlash = function() {
    jQuery("div#streamBoxTable div#streaming_container #streaming").css("visibility", "visible"); 
}





var avodPurchase = new function() {

    var BackoffPoll = function(poll, pollContext, handlers) {
         var onSuccess = handlers.onSuccess;
         var onError = handlers.onError;
         var onTimeout = handlers.onTimeout;

         var iter = 0;
         var MAX_ATTEMPTS = 20;
         var eCount = 0;
         var MAX_ERRORS = 1;

         var getDelay = function() {
             var delay = 0;
             if(iter > 0 && iter < 5) {
                delay = 250 * Math.pow(2, iter - 1);
             } else {
                delay = 4000;
             }
             return delay;
         }

         var retry = function() {
             iter++;
             if(iter < MAX_ATTEMPTS) {
                setTimeout(check , getDelay());
             } else {
                 onTimeout();
             }
         }

         var error = function() {
            if(eCount < MAX_ERRORS) {
                retry();
                eCount++
            } else {
                onError();
            }
         }

         var success = function() {
             onSuccess();
         }

         var check = function() {
             poll(pollContext, retry, success, error);
         }

         this.start = function() {
            check();
         };
     }

    var purchaseTimeout = function(asins, orderID) {
        reload();
        P.when('dv-purchase').execute(function(purchase){
            purchase.purchaseTimeout();
        });
    };
    
    AMZNDetails.purchaseTimeout = purchaseTimeout;

    var purchaseError = function(asins, orderID) {
        reload();
        P.when('dv-purchase').execute(function(purchase){
            purchase.purchaseError(asins);
        });
    }

    var reload = function(asins, orderID, reloadPlayer) {
        var purchasedASINs,
            reloadPlayer = reloadPlayer || true;

        if(typeof asins !== 'undefined') {
          purchasedASINs = {purchasedASINs: asins};
        }

        if(typeof reloadBox === "function") reloadBox(purchasedASINs);
        if(typeof reloadList === "function") reloadList(purchasedASINs);
        if(typeof reloadSeasons === "function") reloadSeasons();

        if (reloadPlayer) {
          try {
            amznJQ.onReady("webGlobalVideoPlayer.MainPlayerInitialized", function() {
              amzn.webGlobalVideoPlayer.getMainPlayer().reload();

              amznJQ.onReady("dvwPlayerContainer", function() {
                amzn.dvwPlayerContainer.refreshPlayerConfig();
              });

            });
          } catch(err) {}
        }
    }


    var showPlaybackWarning = function(asins) {
        P.when('dv-purchase').execute(function(purchase){
            purchase.showPlaybackWarning(asins);
        });
    };

    var warnPlayerRequiredPluginMissing = function(asins) {
        P.when('dv-purchase').execute(function(purchase){
            purchase.warnPlayerRequiredPluginMissing(asins);
        });
    };

    var hdContentWarning = function (asins) {
      P.when('dv-purchase').execute(function(purchase){
          purchase.showHDContentWarning(asins);
      })
    };

    var hdcpContentWarning = function (asins) {
      P.when('dv-purchase').execute(function(purchase){
          purchase.showHDCPContentWarning(asins);
      })
    };

    var doPluginCheck = function(asins) {
        updateStatus("Confirming plugin requirements...");


        var hasRunFlashCheck = false;
        if (hasRunFlashCheck) {
            purchaseContinue(asins);
        }

        amznJQ.onReady("webGlobalVideoPlayer.MainPlayerInitialized", function() {
            if (hasRunFlashCheck) {
                return;
            }
            var mainPlayer = amzn.webGlobalVideoPlayer.getMainPlayer(),
                skipFlashChecks = 0 == 1;

            if (mainPlayer.hasRequiredPluginVersion() || skipFlashChecks) {
                purchaseContinue(asins);
            } else {
                warnPlayerRequiredPluginMissing(asins);
            }
            hasRunFlashCheck = true;
        });

    };

    var showGeoCheck = function(asins) {
        P.when('dv-purchase').execute(function(purchase){
            purchase.showGeoCheck(asins);
        });
    };

    var doGeoCheck = function(asins) {
        updateStatus("Checking location...");
        jQuery.ajax({
            url: "/gp/video/usdvm/order/geo-check.html",
            success: function(data) {
                if(data.success == 1) {
                    purchaseContinue(asins);
                } else {
                    showGeoCheck(asins);
                }
            },
            error: function(a, status) {
                purchaseContinue(asins);
            },
            dataType: "json",
            timeout: 10000
        });
    }

  var skipStage = function(asins){
    purchaseContinue(asins);
  }


  var pinOnPurchase = function(asins) {
      updateStatus("Checking parental control...");
      P.when('dv-purchase').execute(function(dvPurchase){
          dvPurchase.pinCheck(asins);
      });
  }


    var showTVPassWarning = function(asins) {
        P.when('dv-purchase').execute(function(purchase){
            purchase.showTVPassWarning(asins);
        });
    };


    var showBlackoutWarning = function(asins) {
        P.when('dv-purchase').execute(function(purchase){
            purchase.showBlackoutWarning(asins);
        });
    };

    var duplicatePurchase = function(){
        P.when('dv-purchase').execute(function(purchase){
          purchase.duplicatePurchase();
        });
    };


    var canStreamPoll = function(orderID, retry, success, error) {
        jQuery.ajax({
            url: "/gp/video/usdvm/order/check-canstream.html",
            data: {"orderID": orderID},
            success: function(data) {
                if(data) {
                    if(data.canStream === "PENDING") {
                        retry();
                    } else if(data.canStream === "ALLOW") {
                        success();
                    } else {
                        error();
                    }
                } else {
                    error();
                }
            },
            error: function(a, status) {
                if(status === "timeout") {
                    retry();
                } else {
                    error();
                }
            },
            dataType: "json",
            timeout: 10000
        });
    };

    var ajaxPurchase = function(asins) {
        P.when('dv-purchase').execute(function(purchase){
            function ajaxUrl(url, queryParameters) {
                var params = new Array();
                for (key in queryParameters) {
                    params.push(key + '=' + queryParameters[key]);
                }
                var queryString = params.join('&');
                return url + '?' + queryString;
            }

            updateStatus("Purchasing...");


            var secureUrl = "https://www.amazon.com:443/gp/video/usdvm/order/purchase.html/188-0452807-0903467";
            var commonParams = new Object();
            commonParams.ASINS = asins;
            commonParams.sessionID = "188-0452807-0903467";
            commonParams.ref_ = "";

            commonParams.pintoken = encodeURIComponent(purchase.getPinAuthenticationToken(asins));
            if(AMZNDetails && AMZNDetails.csrfToken) {
                commonParams.csrfToken = encodeURIComponent(AMZNDetails.csrfToken);
            };  

            window.handleAvodPurchaseSuccess = function(data) {
                if(data && data.success === "true") {
                   var orderID = data.orderID;
                   purchaseContinue(asins, orderID);
                } else if (data && data.reason === "duplicatePurchase") {
                    avodPurchase.purchaseCancel(asins); 
                    P.when('dv-purchase').execute(function(purchase){
                        purchase.duplicatePurchase();
                    });
                } else if (data && data.reason === "AUTH_REQUIRED" ) {
                  avodPurchase.purchaseCancel(asins);
                  P.when('dv-purchase').execute(function(purchase){
                      purchase.pinAuthenticationFailure();
                  });
                } else {
                   var params = jQuery.extend({"retJSON":"false"}, commonParams);
                   window.location = ajaxUrl(secureUrl, params);
                }
            }
            var head = document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0] || document.documentElement;
            var script = document.createElement("script");
            var params = jQuery.extend({"callback":"handleAvodPurchaseSuccess"}, commonParams);
            script.src = ajaxUrl(secureUrl, params);
            var done = false;

            var timeoutRef = setTimeout(function() {
                if(done) return;
                purchaseTimeout(asins);
             }, 60000);

            script.onload = script.onreadystatechange = function() {
                if ( !done && (!this.readyState || this.readyState === "loaded" || this.readyState === "complete") ) {
                    done = true;

                    clearTimeout(timeoutRef);

                    script.onload = script.onreadystatechange = null;
                    if ( head && script.parentNode ) {
                        head.removeChild( script );
                    }
                }
            };

            var errorHandler = function() {
                done = true;
                clearTimeout(timeoutRef);
                purchaseError(asins);
            };
            script.onerror = errorHandler;
            head.insertBefore( script, head.firstChild );
        });
    }

    var hasRightsPoll = function(asins, retry, success, error) {
        jQuery.ajax({
            url: "/gp/video/usdvm/order/has-rights.html",
            data: {"ASINS": asins},
            success: function(data) {
                if(data) {
                    if(data.hasRights === 'false') {
                        retry();
                    } else if(data.hasRights === 'true') {
                        success();
                    } else {
                        error();
                    }
                } else {
                    error();
                }
            },
            error: function(a, status) {
                if(status === "timeout") {
                    retry();
                } else {
                    error();
                }
            },
            dataType: "json",
            timeout: 10000
        });
    };

    var canStream = function(asins, orderID) {
        updateStatus("Checking order status...");
        var b = new BackoffPoll(canStreamPoll, orderID, {
            onSuccess: function() {
                purchaseContinue(asins);
            },
            onError: function() {
                purchaseError(asins);

                jQuery.ajax({
                    url: "/gp/video/usdvm/pop-overs/error.html",
                    data :
                    {
                      errorA : 0,
                      errorL : 1,
                      page : "DP",
                      data : '{"stage":"canStream","ASINS":"' + asins + '","orderID":"' + orderID + '"}'
                    },
                    type: "POST",
                    timeout: 10000
                });

            },
            onTimeout: function() {
                purchaseTimeout(asins, orderID);
           }
       });
       b.start();
    }

    var hasRights = function(asins) {
        updateStatus("Finalizing rights...");
        var b = new BackoffPoll(hasRightsPoll, asins, {
            onSuccess: function() {
                purchaseContinue(asins);
            },
            onError: function() {
                purchaseError(asins);

                jQuery.ajax({
                    url: "/gp/video/usdvm/pop-overs/error.html",
                    data :
                    {
                      errorA : 0,
                      errorL : 1,
                      page : "DP",
                      data : '{"stage":"hasRights","ASINS":"' + asins + '"}'
                    },
                    type: "POST",
                    timeout: 10000
                });

            },
            onTimeout: function() {
                purchaseTimeout(asins);
            }
        });
        b.start();
    };

    var showAgeVerificationModal = function (asins) {
        updateStatus("Confirming age verification is setup...");
        P.when('dv-fsk18-modal').execute(function (fsk18Modal) {
                fsk18Modal.showAgeVerificationModal(asins);
            }
        );
    };

  var DO_GEO_CHECK = this.DO_GEO_CHECK = "DO_GEO_CHECK";
  var SHOW_BLACKOUT_WARNING = this.SHOW_BLACKOUT_WARNING = "SHOW_BLACKOUT_WARNING";
  var AJAX_PURCHASE = this.AJAX_PURCHASE = "AJAX_PURCHASE";
  var CAN_STREAM = this.CAN_STREAM = "CAN_STREAM";
  var HAS_RIGHTS = this.HAS_RIGHTS = "HAS_RIGHTS";
  var SHOW_AGE_VERIFICATION = this.SHOW_AGE_VERIFICATION = "SHOW_AGE_VERIFICATION";
  var RELOAD = this.RELOAD = "RELOAD";
  var SHOW_TV_PASS_WARNING = this.SHOW_TV_PASS_WARNING = "SHOW_TV_PASS_WARNING";
  var SHOW_PLAYBACK_WARNING = this.SHOW_PLAYBACK_WARNING = "SHOW_PLAYBACK_WARNING";
  var DO_FLASH_CHECK = this.DO_FLASH_CHECK = "DO_FLASH_CHECK";
  var SHOW_HD_CONTENT_WARNING = this.SHOW_HD_CONTENT_WARNING = "SHOW_HD_CONTENT_WARNING";
  var SHOW_HD_CP_CONTENT_WARNING = this.SHOW_HD_CP_CONTENT_WARNING = "SHOW_HD_CP_CONTENT_WARNING";

    var PARENTAL_CONTROL = this.PARENTAL_CONTROL = "PARENTAL_CONTROL";

  var STAGES = {};

  STAGES[DO_GEO_CHECK] = doGeoCheck;
  STAGES[CAN_STREAM] = canStream;
  STAGES[SHOW_BLACKOUT_WARNING] = showBlackoutWarning;
  STAGES[AJAX_PURCHASE] = ajaxPurchase;
  STAGES[HAS_RIGHTS] = hasRights;
  STAGES[RELOAD] = reload;
  STAGES[SHOW_TV_PASS_WARNING] = showTVPassWarning;
  STAGES[SHOW_PLAYBACK_WARNING] = showPlaybackWarning;
  STAGES[DO_FLASH_CHECK] = doPluginCheck;
  STAGES[SHOW_AGE_VERIFICATION] = showAgeVerificationModal;
  STAGES[SHOW_HD_CONTENT_WARNING] = hdContentWarning;
  STAGES[SHOW_HD_CP_CONTENT_WARNING] = hdcpContentWarning;

    STAGES[PARENTAL_CONTROL] = pinOnPurchase;


    var pipeline = {};
  
    var defaultPipeline = [DO_FLASH_CHECK, PARENTAL_CONTROL, DO_GEO_CHECK, AJAX_PURCHASE, CAN_STREAM, HAS_RIGHTS, RELOAD];

pipeline['B004C3DLJS'] = [PARENTAL_CONTROL,AJAX_PURCHASE,CAN_STREAM, HAS_RIGHTS, RELOAD];
pipeline['B005ZMUTZ4'] = [PARENTAL_CONTROL,AJAX_PURCHASE,CAN_STREAM, HAS_RIGHTS, RELOAD];
pipeline['B0094KT9Y0'] = [SHOW_HD_CP_CONTENT_WARNING,PARENTAL_CONTROL,AJAX_PURCHASE,CAN_STREAM, HAS_RIGHTS, RELOAD];
pipeline['B004C3DLJ8'] = [SHOW_HD_CP_CONTENT_WARNING,PARENTAL_CONTROL,AJAX_PURCHASE,CAN_STREAM, HAS_RIGHTS, RELOAD];
var epListStages = "".split(",");
    var stage = {};

    var useEpListStages = false;
    var shownEpListStages = 0;
    var totalEpListStages = 0;
    var purchaseStart = function(asins, epListPurchase) {
        stage[asins] = -1;

        useEpListStages = epListPurchase || false;
        shownEpListStages = 0;

        purchaseContinue(asins);
    }

    var getPipeline = function(asins) {
        var p = pipeline[asins];
        if(!p) {
          if (useEpListStages === true && shownEpListStages < totalEpListStages) {
            p = [];

            for (i in epListStages) {
                p.push(epListStages[i]);
            }

            for (i in defaultPipeline) {
               p.push(defaultPipeline[i]);
            }
            shownEpListStages++;
          } else {
              p = defaultPipeline;
          }
        }

        return p;
    }

    var currentStage = function(asins, context) {
        var i = stage[asins];
        var p = getPipeline(asins);

        var st = p[i];
        var f = STAGES[st];
        if(typeof f === 'function') {
            setTimeout(function() {f(asins, context)}, 1);
        }
    }

    var purchaseContinue = function(asins, context) {
        stage[asins]++;
        currentStage(asins, context);
    }

    var purchaseCancel = function(asins) {
        stage[asins] = -1;

        reload(undefined, undefined, false);
    }

    var purchaseRetry = function(asins, context) {
        setStage(asins, "CAN_STREAM");
        currentStage(asins, context);
    }

    var setStage = function(asins, st) {
        var p = getPipeline(asins);
        for(var i = 0; i < p.length; i++) {
            if(p[i] === st) {
                stage[asins] = i;
                return;
            }
        }
    }

    this.purchaseCancel = purchaseCancel;
    this.purchaseStart = purchaseStart;
    this.purchaseContinue = purchaseContinue;
    this.purchaseRetry = purchaseRetry;
    this.setStage = setStage;
}();

var replaceSideBox = function(ih) {
  var test = jQuery("#dv-side-box-container").html(ih).find(".avod-wrapped-side-box").css("width", "").css("height", "");

    if ( AMZNDetails && AMZNDetails.dvPlayer ) {
        AMZNDetails.dvPlayer.playerButtonsHasChanged();
    }
}

var reloadBox = function(args) {
    var boxArguments = {"*entries*":"0","purchaseBox":"1","*Version*":"1"},
        data = jQuery.extend({}, {"ASIN": "B004C3DLJS"}, args, boxArguments);

    if ( AMZNDetails && AMZNDetails.dvPlayer ) {
        AMZNDetails.dvPlayer.enableTrailer();
    }
    jQuery.ajax({
        url: "/gp/video/widgets/buy-box/ajax/box.html", 
        data: data, 
        success: replaceSideBox,
        error: function() {
            P.when('dv-purchase').execute(function(purchase) {
                purchase.showGenericError("[PURCHASE_FLOW RELOAD BOX FAILED] ASIN : B004C3DLJS" );
            })
        },
        dataType: "html",
        timeout: 10000
    });
}

var showSpinner = function() {
   var $sideBox= jQuery("#avod-side-box");
   var $anchor = $sideBox.find("div.avod-side-box-anchor");
   var spinnerHTML = jQuery("#avod-side-box-spinner").html();
   
   var $table =  $anchor.children(".avod-wrapped-side-box>table");
   
   var w = $table.width();
   var h = Math.max(170, $table.height());
   
   if (spinnerHTML) replaceSideBox(spinnerHTML);
   
   
   if(w !== 0) {
       $anchor.find("table.avod-spritebox")
                    .attr("width", w).attr("height", h);
   }                    
}

    P.when('A','dv-purchase','dv-player').execute(function (A, purchase) {

        var jQuery = A.$;
        // Click purchase buttons have their corresponding asins attached to them
        // We must use undelegate to detach any previous events as when reloadBox gets calls this code gets executed again
        jQuery("body").undelegate(".js-dv-purchase-button","click").delegate(".js-dv-purchase-button", "click", function(e) {
            var self = this;
            showSpinner();
            P.when('ready').execute(function () {
                var $button = jQuery(self),
                    asin = $button.attr('asin'),
                    refTag = jQuery(self).data('reftag');

                if (refTag) sendAnalytics(refTag);
                if ( AMZNDetails && AMZNDetails.dvPlayer && AMZNDetails.dvPlayer.hasPlayer() ) {
                    AMZNDetails.dvPlayer.disableTrailer();
                    AMZNDetails.dvPlayer.close();
                }

                if (!asin) {
                    purchase.showGenericError("[PURCHASE_FLOW MISSING ASIN]");
                    return;
                }

                avodPurchase.purchaseStart(asin);
                return false;
            });
        });

        if (!AMZNDetails.registeredBuyBoxPurchaseButtons) {
            P.register('dv-buybox-purchase-buttons');
        }

        AMZNDetails.registeredBuyBoxPurchaseButtons = true;

    });

<div class="info_box_details">
<div id="player_corrupt_mac_info">
<h1>Silverlight Problem</h1>
<p>There's a problem with the installation of Microsoft Silverlight on your computer. Often, this can be fixed by uninstalling, and then reinstalling Silverlight.</p>
<ol class="player_corrupt_steps_list">
<li>Close all web browser windows, including this one.</li>
<li>Click on the Desktop, or open Finder.</li>
<li>Click <b>Go</b> &gt; <b>Computer</b>.</li>
<li>Double-click <b>Macintosh HD</b> &gt; <b>Library</b> &gt; <b>Internet Plugins</b>.</li>
<li>Drag <b>Silverlight.plugin</b> to the Trash.</li>
<li>Return to this page to install Silverlight.</li>
</ol>
<p class="player_corruption_subdetails">You can also play this video in Adobe Flash player <a href="/gp/product/B004C3DLJS/188-0452807-0903467?ie=UTF8&amp;playertype=flash" onclick="document.getElementById('useFlashForm').submit(); return false;">just this time</a> or for all videos. To change for all videos, on the <a href="/gp/video/ontv/settings" target="_blank">Settings page</a>, in the <b>Player Preferences</b> section, click <b>Adobe Flash Player</b>.</p>
<p class="player_corruption_subdetails">For further assistance, <a href="http://www.amazon.com/gp/help/contact-us/digital-video.html/ref=aiv_ply_sl_gen_err_help">contact Amazon Customer Service</a>.</p>
</div>
<div id="player_corrupt_pc_info">
<h1>Silverlight Problem</h1>
<p>There's a problem with the installation of Microsoft Silverlight on your computer. Microsoft provides a tool that can often fix this problem.</p>
<ol class="player_corrupt_steps_list">
<li><a href="http://download.microsoft.com/download/6/C/9/6C970550-32AB-4235-9CDD-7FC9DD848BBB/silverlight.diagcab" id="player_corrupt_pc_fixit_link">Run the Fix It tool</a></li>
<li>After the tool has completed, refresh this page.</li>
</ol>
<p class="player_corrupt_steps_list">If the Microsoft Fix It Tool fails to fix the problem, try the <a href="#" id="player_corrupt_pc_details_header">Manual Repair Steps</a>.</p>
<div id="player_corrupt_pc_details">
<ol class="player_corrupt_steps_list">
<li>Close all web browser windows, including this one.</li>
<li>Click the Start button, type <b>Uninstall a program</b>, and then press <b>Enter</b>.Windows 8: Swipe in from the right edge of the screen, then tap <b>Settings</b>. You can also press Windows key+I. Select <b>Control Panel</b>, and then select <b>Uninstall a program</b>.</li>
<li>Click <b>Microsoft Silverlight</b>, and then click <b>Uninstall</b>.</li>
<li>Return to this page to install Silverlight.</li>
</ol>
<p class="player_corruption_subdetails">For further assistance, <a href="http://www.amazon.com/gp/help/contact-us/digital-video.html/ref=aiv_ply_sl_gen_err_help">contact Amazon Customer Service</a>.</p>
</div>

var bindAvodAjaxFlyover = function(args) {
    if(typeof amznJQ !== 'undefined') {
        amznJQ.available('popover', function() {
            
            var playerWasVisible = false,
                escapedContent = args.text ? jQuery('<div/>').html(args.text).text() : '';

            jQuery(args.selector).amazonPopoverTrigger({
                showOnHover: true,
                destination: args.url,
                literalContent: escapedContent,
                showCloseButton: false,
                width: args.width,
                location: args.location,
	           alignMargin: '20',
                ajaxErrorContent: '<p>We encountered a problem. Please try again.</p>',
                onShow: function() {
                    // hide player if present
                    if (args.pausePlayer == 1) {
                        amznJQ.onReady("webGlobalVideoPlayer.MainPlayerInitialized", function() {
                            amznJQ.onReady("dvwPlayerContainer", function() {
                                var mainPlayer = amzn.webGlobalVideoPlayer.getMainPlayer();
                                if (mainPlayer.isVisible()) {
                                   playerWasVisible = true;
                                    mainPlayer.close();
                                }
                            });
                        });
                    }
                },
                skin :   function(){ 
                return  '<div class="aiv-dv-popover-aui">' +
                            '<div class="a-popover a-popover-modal">' + 
                                '<div class="a-popover-wrapper">' + 
                                    '<div class="a-popover-header">' + 
                                        '<div class="ap_title"></div>' +
                                    '</div>' +
                                        '<div class="ap_content"></div>' + 
                                '</div>' + 
                            '</div>' + 
                        '</div>'
                    },
                onHide: function() {
                    // show player and restart playback if needed                      
                    amznJQ.onReady("webGlobalVideoPlayer.MainPlayerInitialized", function() {
                        amznJQ.onReady("dvwPlayerContainer", function() {
                            var mainPlayer = amzn.webGlobalVideoPlayer.getMainPlayer();
                            if (playerWasVisible) {
                                mainPlayer.play();
                            }
                        });
                    });
                },
                closeEventInclude: "MOUSE_LEAVE"
            });
        });
    }
}

                escapedContent = args.text ? jQuery('<div/>').html(args.text).text() : '';

            var amznAIV = window.amznAIV || {};
            amznAIV.aivPopOver = jQuery.AmazonPopover.displayPopover({

                        + '<div id="avod-error-box" align="center"><table class="avod-spritebox avod-cancel-button ap_custom_close" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0">  <tr height="19">    <td class="content" style="vertical-align: bottom;  ; background: url(http://g-ecx.images-amazon.com/images/G/01/digital/video/avod-1-5/dp-sprite-total._V156422041_.png) no-repeat -3px -153px; padding: 0px 4px 0px 11px;">      OK    </td>    <td width="7" style="vertical-align: bottom;  ; background: url(http://g-ecx.images-amazon.com/images/G/01/digital/video/avod-1-5/dp-sprite-total._V156422041_.png) no-repeat -396px -153px; line-height: 0.1px;"><!-- --></td>  </tr>  <tr height="7">    <td style="vertical-align: bottom;  ; background: url(http://g-ecx.images-amazon.com/images/G/01/digital/video/avod-1-5/dp-sprite-total._V156422041_.png) no-repeat -3px -174px"></td>    <td width="7" style="vertical-align: bottom;  ; background: url(http://g-ecx.images-amazon.com/images/G/01/digital/video/avod-1-5/dp-sprite-total._V156422041_.png) no-repeat -396px -174px; line-height: 0.1px;"><!-- --></td>  </tr></table></div>',

                            var mainPlayer = amzn.webGlobalVideoPlayer.getMainPlayer();

                                playerWasVisible = true;
                                mainPlayer.close();
                            }
                        });
                    });
                },
                onHide: function() {
                    // show player and restart playback if needed
                    amznJQ.onReady("webGlobalVideoPlayer.MainPlayerInitialized", function() {
                        amznJQ.onReady("dvwPlayerContainer", function() {
                            var mainPlayer = amzn.webGlobalVideoPlayer.getMainPlayer();

}
var showAvodAjaxPurchaseDialog = function(args, asins) {
                
    var playerWasVisible = false,
        escapedContent = args.text ? jQuery('<div/>').html(args.text).text() : '';

    jQuery.AmazonPopover.displayPopover({
        title: '<h4>' + args.title + '</h4>',
        destination: args.url,
        literalContent: escapedContent,
        loadingContent: "<div class='avod-pop-loader'></div>",
        ajaxTimeout:10000, 
        ajaxErrorContent: '<p>We encountered a problem. Please try again.</p>'
                        + '<div id="avod-error-box" align="center"><table class="avod-spritebox avod-cancel-button ap_custom_close" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0">  <tr height="19">    <td class="content" style="vertical-align: bottom;  ; background: url(http://g-ecx.images-amazon.com/images/G/01/digital/video/avod-1-5/dp-sprite-total._V156422041_.png) no-repeat -3px -153px; padding: 0px 4px 0px 11px;">      OK    </td>    <td width="7" style="vertical-align: bottom;  ; background: url(http://g-ecx.images-amazon.com/images/G/01/digital/video/avod-1-5/dp-sprite-total._V156422041_.png) no-repeat -396px -153px; line-height: 0.1px;"><!-- --></td>  </tr>  <tr height="7">    <td style="vertical-align: bottom;  ; background: url(http://g-ecx.images-amazon.com/images/G/01/digital/video/avod-1-5/dp-sprite-total._V156422041_.png) no-repeat -3px -174px"></td>    <td width="7" style="vertical-align: bottom;  ; background: url(http://g-ecx.images-amazon.com/images/G/01/digital/video/avod-1-5/dp-sprite-total._V156422041_.png) no-repeat -396px -174px; line-height: 0.1px;"><!-- --></td>  </tr></table></div>' +    
                                '<SCR' + 'IPT TYPE="TEXT/JAVSCRIPT">' +
                                '   jQuery("#avod-error-box")'     +
                                '       .find(".avod-cancel-button")' +
                                '       .click(function() {'    +
                                '          avodPurchase.purchaseCancel("' + asins + '");' +
                                '       });'+
                                '</SCR' + 'IPT>',
        width:600,
        showCloseButton: false,
        group:"avod-popover",
        closeEventExclude: "CLICK_OUTSIDE",
        onShow: function() {
            // hide player if present
            amznJQ.onReady("webGlobalVideoPlayer.MainPlayerInitialized", function() {
                amznJQ.onReady("dvwPlayerContainer", function() {
                    var mainPlayer = amzn.webGlobalVideoPlayer.getMainPlayer();
                    if (mainPlayer.isVisible()) {
                        playerWasVisible = true;
                        mainPlayer.close();
                    }
                });
            });
        },
        onHide: function() {
            // show player and restart playback if needed
            amznJQ.onReady("webGlobalVideoPlayer.MainPlayerInitialized", function() {
                amznJQ.onReady("dvwPlayerContainer", function() {
                    var mainPlayer = amzn.webGlobalVideoPlayer.getMainPlayer();
                    if (playerWasVisible) {
                        mainPlayer.play();
                    }
                });
            });
        },
        skin :   function(){ 
        return  '<div class="aiv-dv-popover-aui">' +
                    '<div class="a-popover a-popover-modal">' + 
                        '<div class="a-popover-wrapper">' +

        modal:true,

    });

<h3 class="a-spacing-small">Most Helpful Customer Reviews</h3>
<div class="a-section" id="revMHRL">
<div class="a-section celwidget" id="rev-dpReviewsMostHelpfulAUI-RHBBXRODROY7M"><div class="a-row a-spacing-micro"><span class="a-size-small a-color-secondary">182 of 203 people found the following review helpful</span><div class="a-icon-row a-spacing-none"><a class="a-link-normal a-text-normal a-color-base" href="http://www.amazon.com/review/RHBBXRODROY7M/ref=cm_cr_dp_title/188-0452807-0903467?ie=UTF8&amp;ASIN=B004C3DLJS&amp;nodeID=2858778011&amp;store=instant-video" title="5.0 out of 5 stars"><i class="a-icon a-icon-star a-star-5"></i></a><span class="a-letter-space"></span><a class="a-link-normal a-text-normal a-color-base" href="http://www.amazon.com/review/RHBBXRODROY7M/ref=cm_cr_dp_title/188-0452807-0903467?ie=UTF8&amp;ASIN=B004C3DLJS&amp;nodeID=2858778011&amp;store=instant-video"><span class="a-size-base a-text-bold">Nostalgia in a big, big way</span></a></div><span class="a-color-secondary">
<span class="a-size-normal">
<span class="a-color-secondary">
      By
    </span>
<a class="noTextDecoration" href="/gp/pdp/profile/A32XGYDA14KT13/ref=cm_cr_dp_pdp/188-0452807-0903467">A book lover in Azle Texas</a>
</span>
<span class="a-declarative" data-action="cr-popup" data-cr-popup='{"width":340,"title":"AmazonHelp","height":340}' style="display:inline;"><span class="a-size-micro"><a class="a-link-normal a-text-normal" href="http://www.amazon.com/gp/help/customer/display.html/ref=cm_cr_dp_bdg_help/188-0452807-0903467?ie=UTF8&amp;nodeId=14279681&amp;pop-up=1#vn"><span class="a-color-link c7yBadgeAUI c7yTopDownDashedStrike a-text-bold">VINE VOICE</span></a></span></span><span class="a-color-secondary"> on October 27, 2010</span></span></div><div class="a-row a-spacing-small" id="revData-dpReviewsMostHelpfulAUI-RHBBXRODROY7M"><span class="a-size-mini a-color-secondary">Format: Blu-ray<i class="a-icon a-icon-text-separator"></i></span><span class="a-size-mini a-color-state a-text-bold">
    Verified Purchase
  </span>
<div class="a-section">
  My review is brief as others have almost said it all.  I just want to say that I am 62 years old, and just the thought about the way I felt when I saw this movie in the theatre makes me tear up.  It is a nostalgic feeling in a big way.  Reminds you of your childhood and those special feelings about growing up.  You want to grow up and get on to being an adult in the worst way, but thinking back now your childhood was such a very special time.  So fleeting and if we're lucky, such a special time in our lives.<br>I highly recommend the purchase of this movie to add to your collection.<br>I honestly feel that the series should stop here.  Perfect right where it was left.
</br></br></div>

<div class="a-section celwidget" id="rev-dpReviewsMostHelpfulAUI-R2VO8TYC6B1MNN"><div class="a-row a-spacing-micro"><span class="a-size-small a-color-secondary">169 of 213 people found the following review helpful</span><div class="a-icon-row a-spacing-none"><a class="a-link-normal a-text-normal a-color-base" href="http://www.amazon.com/review/R2VO8TYC6B1MNN/ref=cm_cr_dp_title/188-0452807-0903467?ie=UTF8&amp;ASIN=B004C3DLJS&amp;nodeID=2858778011&amp;store=instant-video" title="5.0 out of 5 stars"><i class="a-icon a-icon-star a-star-5"></i></a><span class="a-letter-space"></span><a class="a-link-normal a-text-normal a-color-base" href="http://www.amazon.com/review/R2VO8TYC6B1MNN/ref=cm_cr_dp_title/188-0452807-0903467?ie=UTF8&amp;ASIN=B004C3DLJS&amp;nodeID=2858778011&amp;store=instant-video"><span class="a-size-base a-text-bold">A worthy completion of a classic trilogy</span></a></div><span class="a-color-secondary">
<span class="a-size-normal">
<span class="a-color-secondary">
      By
    </span>
<a class="noTextDecoration" href="/gp/pdp/profile/A1V3TRGWOMA8LC/ref=cm_cr_dp_pdp/188-0452807-0903467">James Beswick</a>
</span>
<span class="a-declarative" data-action="cr-popup" data-cr-popup='{"width":340,"title":"AmazonHelp","height":340}' style="display:inline;"><span class="a-size-micro"><a class="a-link-normal a-text-normal" href="http://www.amazon.com/gp/help/customer/display.html/ref=cm_cr_dp_bdg_help/188-0452807-0903467?ie=UTF8&amp;nodeId=14279681&amp;pop-up=1#vn"><span class="a-color-link c7yBadgeAUI c7yTopDownDashedStrike a-text-bold">VINE VOICE</span></a></span></span><span class="a-color-secondary"> on June 12, 2010</span></span></div><div class="a-row a-spacing-small" id="revData-dpReviewsMostHelpfulAUI-R2VO8TYC6B1MNN"><span class="a-size-mini a-color-secondary">Format: DVD</span>
<div class="a-section">
<span class="MHRHead">I went to the San Francisco Film Festival screening at Pixar Studios last night not really knowing what to expect. Toy Story has been with us for 15 years now (20, in terms of actual development) and I had a sinking feeling that maybe all the character potential had been used in the first two and this was some shameless plot by Disney to exploit the franchise ("Little Mermaid 3", anyone?). Well, shame on me for underestimating the capabilities of Pixar, who once again have shown how a small studio in Emeryville is a storytelling powerhouse that leaves the rest of the industry in the dust.<br><br>Toy Story 3 is the tale of Andy, the toys' owner, going to college and their quest to determine their future - headed between the attic or a daycare center. If you've enjoyed the way the first two films blend character drama with innovative action and humor, this cocktail hits its stride in the third film, which draws on everything we already know about the characters and then adds two new entire sets of toys to the plot. There's a new villain, two very amusing romance sub-plots and a litany of visual gags that push the envelope even further. I'm not allowed to go into any details but the second half of the film is a familiar set piece performed in a completely new way that will forever change your view of certain toys and day care centers.<br><br>Apart from a level of animation that sets the bar in the industry and an attention to detail that makes you wonder what most "real" films actually do in pre-production, the real genius of the third film is to provide a satisfying conclusion that gives every character a completed character arc.</br></br></br></br></span><span class="a-declarative" data-action="columnbalancing-showfullreview" data-columnbalancing-showfullreview="{&quot;rest&quot;:&quot; About 20 minutes before the end, I was wondering how they would do this since there were some fairly dark moments (similar to those in Wall-E and Up), but naturally they manage to pull it together. There's literally not a single wasted shot, let alone a wasted scene, and the pace quickens throughout to keep the tension mounting.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Overall, this is another Pixar classic that easily has enough for both kids and adults (and movie aficionados). It's not difficult to see why each of their movies takes five years to complete - yet despite the technical wizardry, the success of their movies is fundamentally routed in their stories, a fact which most other studios seem to forget these days. As to whether the stage is set for Toy Story 4, I suppose they could always pull it off given the creativity at work here, but I think there was a deliberate attempt to make this the last in the series.&quot;}"><a class="a-link-normal" href="http://www.amazon.com/Toy-Story-3-Tom-Hanks/product-reviews/B004C3DLJS/ref=cm_cr_dp_text/188-0452807-0903467?ie=UTF8&amp;showViewpoints=0&amp;sortBy=byRankDescending#R2VO8TYC6B1MNN"><span class="a-letter-space"></span>Read more ›</a></span>
</div>
</div>

<div class="a-section celwidget" id="rev-dpReviewsMostHelpfulAUI-R3II5AJH95KT59"><div class="a-row a-spacing-micro"><span class="a-size-small a-color-secondary">149 of 194 people found the following review helpful</span><div class="a-icon-row a-spacing-none"><a class="a-link-normal a-text-normal a-color-base" href="http://www.amazon.com/review/R3II5AJH95KT59/ref=cm_cr_dp_title/188-0452807-0903467?ie=UTF8&amp;ASIN=B004C3DLJS&amp;nodeID=2858778011&amp;store=instant-video" title="5.0 out of 5 stars"><i class="a-icon a-icon-star a-star-5"></i></a><span class="a-letter-space"></span><a class="a-link-normal a-text-normal a-color-base" href="http://www.amazon.com/review/R3II5AJH95KT59/ref=cm_cr_dp_title/188-0452807-0903467?ie=UTF8&amp;ASIN=B004C3DLJS&amp;nodeID=2858778011&amp;store=instant-video"><span class="a-size-base a-text-bold">No owners means no heartbreak</span></a></div><span class="a-color-secondary">
<span class="a-size-normal">
<span class="a-color-secondary">
      By
    </span>
<a class="noTextDecoration" href="/gp/pdp/profile/A1D2C0WDCSHUWZ/ref=cm_cr_dp_pdp/188-0452807-0903467">E. A Solinas</a>
</span>
<span class="a-declarative" data-action="cr-popup" data-cr-popup='{"width":340,"title":"AmazonHelp","height":340}' style="display:inline;"><span class="a-size-micro"><a class="a-link-normal a-text-normal" href="http://www.amazon.com/gp/help/customer/display.html/ref=cm_cr_dp_bdg_help/188-0452807-0903467?ie=UTF8&amp;nodeId=14279681&amp;pop-up=1#hf"><span class="a-color-link c7yBadgeAUI c7yTopDownDashedStrike a-text-bold">HALL OF FAME</span></a></span><span class="a-letter-space"></span><span class="a-letter-space"></span><span class="a-size-micro"><a class="a-link-normal a-text-normal" href="http://www.amazon.com/gp/help/customer/display.html/ref=cm_cr_dp_bdg_help/188-0452807-0903467?ie=UTF8&amp;nodeId=14279681&amp;pop-up=1#tr"><span class="a-color-link c7yBadgeAUI c7yTopDownDashedStrike a-text-bold">TOP 100 REVIEWER</span></a></span><span class="a-letter-space"></span><span class="a-letter-space"></span><span class="a-size-micro"><a class="a-link-normal a-text-normal" href="http://www.amazon.com/gp/help/customer/display.html/ref=cm_cr_dp_bdg_help/188-0452807-0903467?ie=UTF8&amp;nodeId=14279681&amp;pop-up=1#vn"><span class="a-color-link c7yBadgeAUI c7yTopDownDashedStrike a-text-bold">VINE VOICE</span></a></span></span><span class="a-color-secondary"> on August 12, 2010</span></span></div><div class="a-row a-spacing-small" id="revData-dpReviewsMostHelpfulAUI-R3II5AJH95KT59"><span class="a-size-mini a-color-secondary">Format: Blu-ray</span>
<div class="a-section">
<span class="MHRHead">"Toy Story" was about sibling rivalry. "Toy Story 2" was about loving others, even if it means you might get hurt someday.<br><br>So what is "Toy Story 3" about? It takes the whole "kids + loyal toys" theme to its natural conclusion, by showing us what happens when the kids grow up and leave. While the first two-thirds of the movie are fairly pedestrian (for a Pixar movie!), the last part is both action-packed and emotionally wrenching.<br><br>Ten years have passed, and Andy is now a college-bound teenager. His toys are anxious about what's going to happen, so Woody keeps assuring them that they'll be put safely in the attic. But a misunderstanding leads to a date with the garbage truck. Since the toys believe they have been abandoned, they jump into the box of donated toys bound for Sunnyside Daycare.<br><br>They're greeted by the genial Lots-o'-Hugging Bear (aka Lotso) and the friendly daycare toys, and all seems to be well. But Andy's toys soon discover that Sunnyside is a nighmare -- they've been assigned the "Caterpillar Room" for wild abusive toddlers, and Lotso is the Godfatheresque overlord of the daycare. Once Woody learns the true horrors of Sunnyside, he must infiltrate the daycare and somehow get his friends out.<br><br>You know that the movie industry is officially in a slump when the cleverest, funniest and most touching movie of the summer... is a CGI sequel about toys. "Toy Story 3" starts off rather lightweight at first, with the toys being brought into Sunnyside and Woody setting off in another direction.<br><br>But once Lotso is revealed as the villain, the movie takes a sharp turn -- it becomes a clever, complex "Great Escape"-style caper, with some moments of G-rated horror (THE MONKEY!</br></br></br></br></br></br></br></br></br></br></span><span class="a-declarative" data-action="columnbalancing-showfullreview" data-columnbalancing-showfullreview="{&quot;rest&quot;:&quot;) and hilarity (resetting Buzz ends up turning him into a flamenco-dancing suave Spaniard). And while the toys' attempted escape from Sunnyside is taut and genuinely thrilling, it's only the START of the climax -- a harrowing, genuinely scary chase scene that brings the toys together.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;And there's a bittersweet core to \&quot;Toy Story 3\&quot;: kids grow up, leave home and the people/toys they leave behind are both proud and sad. In the final scenes of the movie,we're quietly ushered through the emotional goodbyes and hellos of growing up.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;And the adorable little cast of toys still remind us that what matters most is love and loyalty, particularly during a deadly crisis where they all fearfully join hands (it sounds sappy, but it isn't). There's also some endearing additions to the cast -- the foppish clotheshorse Ken, Big Baby, a Totoro, a giggly tricerotops, and the Shakespearean stuffed hedgehog Mr. Pricklepants.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Anyway, this blu-ray/DVD combo has a wealth of extras -- trailers teasers, theatrical shorts (oh look, Night and Day are scuffling!), \&quot;Cine-emplore,\&quot; commentary, lots of making-ofs, behind the scenes stuff like \&quot;A Toy's Eye View: Creating A Whole New Land,\&quot; a music video, and just lots of endearing odds and ends like Ken's dating tips. Er...&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;It hurts to say goodbye to Woody, Buzz and their friends, but \&quot;Toy Story 3\&quot; is a fitting farewell that brings the trilogy full circle. Best movie of the summer, hands down.&quot;}"><a class="a-link-normal" href="http://www.amazon.com/Toy-Story-3-Tom-Hanks/product-reviews/B004C3DLJS/ref=cm_cr_dp_text/188-0452807-0903467?ie=UTF8&amp;showViewpoints=0&amp;sortBy=byRankDescending#R3II5AJH95KT59"><span class="a-letter-space"></span>Read more ›</a></span>
</div>

<div class="a-section celwidget" id="rev-dpReviewsMostHelpfulAUI-R3MIQT2BX05RMR"><div class="a-row a-spacing-micro"><span class="a-size-small a-color-secondary">9 of 10 people found the following review helpful</span><div class="a-icon-row a-spacing-none"><a class="a-link-normal a-text-normal a-color-base" href="http://www.amazon.com/review/R3MIQT2BX05RMR/ref=cm_cr_dp_title/188-0452807-0903467?ie=UTF8&amp;ASIN=B004C3DLJS&amp;nodeID=2858778011&amp;store=instant-video" title="4.0 out of 5 stars"><i class="a-icon a-icon-star a-star-4"></i></a><span class="a-letter-space"></span><a class="a-link-normal a-text-normal a-color-base" href="http://www.amazon.com/review/R3MIQT2BX05RMR/ref=cm_cr_dp_title/188-0452807-0903467?ie=UTF8&amp;ASIN=B004C3DLJS&amp;nodeID=2858778011&amp;store=instant-video"><span class="a-size-base a-text-bold">WORTH THE WAIT</span></a></div><span class="a-color-secondary">
<span class="a-size-normal">
<span class="a-color-secondary">
      By
    </span>
<a class="noTextDecoration" href="/gp/pdp/profile/A18S2VGUH9SCV5/ref=cm_cr_dp_pdp/188-0452807-0903467">Margaux Paschke</a>
</span>
<span class="a-declarative" data-action="cr-popup" data-cr-popup='{"width":340,"title":"AmazonHelp","height":340}' style="display:inline;"><span class="a-size-micro"><a class="a-link-normal a-text-normal" href="http://www.amazon.com/gp/help/customer/display.html/ref=cm_cr_dp_bdg_help/188-0452807-0903467?ie=UTF8&amp;nodeId=14279681&amp;pop-up=1#vn"><span class="a-color-link c7yBadgeAUI c7yTopDownDashedStrike a-text-bold">VINE VOICE</span></a></span></span><span class="a-color-secondary"> on June 21, 2010</span></span></div><div class="a-row a-spacing-small" id="revData-dpReviewsMostHelpfulAUI-R3MIQT2BX05RMR"><span class="a-size-mini a-color-secondary">Format: DVD</span>
<div class="a-section">
<span class="MHRHead">This third Toy Story was a winner.  The story is a great continuation that spoke to my older son as he outgrows his once beloved Woody &amp; Buzz and still fascinates my younger one.<br><br>This movie centers around Andy, all grown up, going away to college and having to clean out his bedroom.  Should he donate his old toys? Throw them out?  Or keep them in the attic for his children?  Woody, Buzz and a few other toys that have survived over the years try one last time to get Andy to play with them.  Their failure makes them think they are doomed for the trash pile and rather then suffer this horrible fate, they plot to get into the donate box. Woody insists that Andy intends for them to be stored in the attic but the others do not believe him.<br><br>Their arrival at Sunnyside playschool makes them think they've hit the jackpot but all is not as rosy as it seems.  There is a dark undercurrent here, lead by a strawberry smelling stuffed bear.  This brought cries of horror from my youngest along with lots of questions.  Did that mean the toys we donated were being treated horribly too?  Although it all ends well, this part stuck with my youngest.  I sense trouble the next time I attempt to clean out his closet by donating toys he has outgrown.  Thanks Disney.<br><br>This movie attempts to cater to all age groups.  The parents will need a tissue as it pulls at the heartstrings.  From start, by showing a home movie of Andy when he was young and flashing to present day at a teenage Andy gets ready for college, to finish as the mom looks around Andy's empty room.  Her child is leaving home.  It speaks to tweens who want to leave childish things behind but still have great affection for childhood toys.  The appeal to young kids is as strong as ever as we follow the adventures of Woody and Buzz.</br></br></br></br></br></br></span><span class="a-declarative" data-action="columnbalancing-showfullreview" data-columnbalancing-showfullreview="{&quot;rest&quot;:&quot;  It did contain another creepy baby to give some nightmares.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;There were some mature references for a \&quot;G\&quot; rated movie.  Ken being gay was referenced several times and they had him striking sexy poses.  They had Buzz set to Spanish mode where he spoke Spanish for a minute or two.  The scene was funny to me but the subtitles annoyed my youngest as he couldn't keep up.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;This movie told a great tale of getting older for those kids who grew up with Woody and Buzz.  Both my boys could not stop talking about it afterwards.  I would skip the 3D version as nothing in the film warrants the use of 3D.&quot;}"><a class="a-link-normal" href="http://www.amazon.com/Toy-Story-3-Tom-Hanks/product-reviews/B004C3DLJS/ref=cm_cr_dp_text/188-0452807-0903467?ie=UTF8&amp;showViewpoints=0&amp;sortBy=byRankDescending#R3MIQT2BX05RMR"><span class="a-letter-space"></span>Read more ›</a></span>
</div>
</div>

P.when("A").execute(function(A) {
   
   function vote(event) {
     var root = A.$(event.data.rootComponentId);
     var target = event.$target;
     root.find(".cr-vote-buttons").addClass("a-hidden");
     root.find(".cr-vote-feedback").removeClass("a-hidden");
       
     A.get(target.attr("href") + "&type=json&_=" + (new Date()).getTime(),
     {
	   dataType: 'json',
	   ajaxTimeout: 10000,
	   success: function(data, textStatus){ 
         success(data, root, target);
       },
	   error: function(XMLHttpRequest, textStatus, errorThrown){
         error(root, target);
       }
	 });
     event.$event.preventDefault();

   }

   function isNoButton(target) {       
     return target.closest(".noButton").length > 0;
   }

   function success(data, root, target) {
       if (data.redirect == 1) {
	   window.location.href = target.attr("href");
       } else if (data.error == 1) {
	   error(root, target);
       } else {
	   if (isNoButton(target)) {
               root.find(".cr-vote-inapp").removeClass("a-hidden");
	   }
	   root.find(".cr-vote-success").removeClass("a-hidden");	   
	   root.find(".cr-vote-feedback").addClass("a-hidden");
       }
   }

   function error(root, target) {
       root.find(".cr-vote-error").removeClass("a-hidden");	   
       root.find(".cr-vote-feedback").addClass("a-hidden");
   }

   A.declarative("cr-vote", ["click"], vote);
});
